Drag a root view controller from the library into this navigation controller. Set the class of the root controller in the identity inspector. In the attributes inspector specify the name of a xib file that contains the view for the root view controller.
In that xib file, set the File's Owner's custom class to match the root controller and connect the File's Owner's "view" outlet to a top level view.
